=== SHEET MAPPING ===
s1-as = Assumptions & Inputs
s2-sf = SF Breakdown
s3-so = Sources & Uses
s4-mo = Monthly PF Cash Flow
s5-pr = Pro Forma (Annual)
s6-un = Untrended Pro Forma
s7-in = Investor Returns - Pari Passu
s8-in = Investor Returns - Sep Pref Pay
s9-bu = Budget to Convert Existing Bldg
s10-bu = Budget for New Bldg
s11-pr = Property Data
s12-re = Rental Income Model
s13-ye = 5 Year Model
s14-ye = 5 Year Summary
s15-re = RE Tax UW
s16-co = Comps
